<div><img title="Kimber" src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/kimber/dept/Kimber-865x275.jpg" alt="Kimber" width="865" height="275"></div> <div style="float: left; margin: 12px 12px 0px 0px;"><a href="../kimber-new-guns-2015.aspx"><img title="Kimber New Guns" src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/kimber/dept/New-Guns-280x135.jpg" alt="Kimber New Guns" width="280" height="135"></a></div> <div style="float: left; margin: 12px 12px 0px 0px;"><a href="../kimber-handguns.aspx"><img title="Kimber Handguns" style="clear: both; padding-top: 10px;"> <p>Kimber was established for the sole purpose of building the world's finest custom guns. It all started with the Kimber Custom, the 1911 that all other 1911 guns are compared against today. Kimber Pro Carry 1911's are some of the most sought-after concealed carry gun models on the market for their quality, craftsmanship and price. The Kimber Gold Combat chambered in 45 ACP is the gold standard of custom carry full-size 1911s. Kimber uses only the finest parts in their custom pistols, including: night sights, Kimber magazines, cocobolo or black grips, match grade stainless steel barrel, crimson trace laser grips on select pistol models, stainless steel slide, and a host of 1911 accessories. If you're looking for a compact 1911, check out the Kimber Ultra Carry, the original subcompact pistol. If you're looking for a crimson trace laser equipped gun, look at the Kimber Pro Crimson Carry with a black contoured slide, crimson trace laser grips and capable of handling today's defense ammo. The ultimate custom carry pistol, the Kimber Super Carry Pro comes with night sights, stainless steel black slide, and a host of features only Kimber can offer. Impact Guns is a Kimber Master Dealer and we take pride in the Kimber pistols that we sell.</p> </div></span></div> <div style="margin-left:20px;"> <div id="dept-banner" style="margin-bottom:14px;
